[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Stress at work:

**Stress at Work Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to understand your experiences and perceptions of stress at work. Your responses will help us identify areas where we can improve our work environment and support your well-being. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to elaborate on your responses if you'd like.

**Section 1: General Information**

1. What is your current job title and department?
2. How many years have you been working at our company?
3. What are your typical working hours (e.g., 9-to-5, flexible, etc.)?

**Section 2: Perceived Stress Levels**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how would you rate your overall stress level at work (1 = very low, 5 = very high)?
2. Which of the following statements best describes your current stress level?
	* I feel overwhelmed and struggling to cope
	* I feel moderately stressed, but manageable
	* I feel slightly stressed, but okay
	* I feel very little stress
3. Have you experienced any significant changes in your workload or responsibilities recently? If yes, please describe.

**Section 3: Stressors at Work**

1. Which of the following work-related factors contributes most to your stress (select up to 3)?
	* Excessive workload or deadlines
	* Lack of control or autonomy
	* Conflicting priorities or multiple tasks
	* Unclear expectations or unclear roles
	* Poor communication or lack of feedback
	* Other (please specify)
2. Are there any specific situations or events that trigger your stress at work? If yes, please describe.

**Section 4: Coping Mechanisms**

1. How do you typically cope with stress at work? (Select up to 2)
	* Taking regular breaks or time off
	* Seeking support from colleagues or supervisors
	* Engaging in relaxation techniques (e.g., meditation, deep breathing)
	* Focusing on the task at hand and pushing through
	* Other (please specify)
2. Have you noticed any changes in your physical or emotional well-being due to stress at work? If yes, please describe.

**Section 5: Suggestions for Improvement**

1. What changes or initiatives would you suggest to reduce stress at work?
2. Are there any specific resources or support systems you would like to see implemented to help manage stress?

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your input is invaluable in helping us understand stress at work and identifying areas for improvement. If you have any additional comments or suggestions, please feel free to include them below.

Please let me know if you'd like me to convert this questionnaire into a specific format (e.g., Google Forms, Excel, etc.)!

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current workplace environment?

(1 = Very Dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Satisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)

2. What do you like most about your workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

3. What do you like least about your workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 2: Physical Workspace**

4. How would you rate the overall cleanliness and organization of your workspace?

(1 = Poor, 2 = Fair, 3 = Good, 4 = Excellent, 5 = Outstanding)

5. Are there any physical aspects of your workspace that you find distracting or uncomfortable? If yes, please specify.

(Open-ended text field)

6. Do you have a dedicated workspace or shared workspace? If shared, how do you feel about it?

(1 = Love it, 2 = It's okay, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Dislike it, 5 = Hate it)

**Section 3: Social and Cultural Environment**

7. How would you rate the overall morale and camaraderie among colleagues?

(1 = Poor, 2 = Fair, 3 = Good, 4 = Excellent, 5 = Outstanding)

8. Are there any social or cultural aspects of your workplace that you find unwelcoming or uninclusive? If yes, please specify.

(Open-ended text field)

9. Do you feel like your opinions and ideas are valued and respected in the workplace?

(1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)

**Section 4: Technology and Tools**

10. How would you rate the effectiveness of our technology and tools in supporting your work?

(1 = Poor, 2 = Fair, 3 = Good, 4 = Excellent, 5 = Outstanding)

11. Are there any technology or tool-related issues that you experience regularly? If yes, please specify.

(Open-ended text field)

12. Do you feel like you have the necessary training and support to effectively use our technology and tools?

(1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

13. Is there anything else you'd like to share about your workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey! Your feedback is greatly appreciated.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a questionnaire on Remote working experience:

**Remote Working Experience Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As we continue to navigate the new normal of remote work, we want to understand your experiences and challenges. Your feedback will help us improve our remote work policies and practices. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**Section 1: General Experience**

1. How often do you work remotely?
	* Daily
	* Several times a week
	* Occasionally
	* Rarely
2. What is your primary reason for working remotely?
	* Flexibility and work-life balance
	* Reduced commuting time and expenses
	* Improved productivity and focus
	* Other (please specify)
3. How would you rate your overall experience with remote work?
	* Very positive
	* Somewhat positive
	* Neutral
	* Somewhat negative
	* Very negative

**Section 2: Productivity and Focus**

4. Do you find it easier or harder to stay focused and productive while working remotely?
	* Easier
	* Same
	* Harder
5. What are the most significant distractions you face while working remotely?
	* Family members or roommates
	* Social media and online browsing
	* Email notifications and messaging apps
	* Other (please specify)
6. How do you currently manage your work hours and schedule while working remotely?
	* I set a specific schedule and stick to it
	* I have a general idea of my work hours, but flexibility is key
	* I don't have a set schedule, and my work hours vary

**Section 3: Communication and Collaboration**

7. How do you currently communicate with your team and manager while working remotely?
	* Video conferencing (e.g., Zoom, Google Meet)
	* Phone calls
	* Email and messaging apps
	* In-person meetings (when possible)
8. Have you experienced any challenges with communication or collaboration while working remotely?
	* Yes
	* No
9. If yes, what are the most significant challenges you face?
	* Technical issues with video conferencing or online tools
	* Difficulty reading tone and facial expressions in digital communication
	* Lack of face-to-face interactions and social connections
	* Other (please specify)

**Section 4: Support and Resources**

10. Do you feel supported and equipped with the necessary resources to work effectively while working remotely?
	* Yes
	* Mostly
	* Somewhat
	* Not at all
11. What additional resources or support would you like to see implemented to enhance your remote work experience?
	* Training and guidance on remote work best practices
	* Access to virtual collaboration tools and platforms
	* Regular check-ins and feedback from managers
	* Other (please specify)

**Section 5: Additional Comments and Suggestions**

12. Do you have any additional comments or suggestions about your remote working experience?
	* (Open-ended text field for respondents to provide feedback)

Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and experiences with us! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our remote work practices.

**End of Working Relationship Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to gather feedback and insights on the end of working relationship between [Company Name] and [Employee Name]. Your responses will help us improve our processes and provide a better experience for our employees.

**Section 1: Overall Experience**

1. How would you rate your overall experience with [Company Name] during your employment?

a) Very positive
b) Somewhat positive
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat negative
e) Very negative

2. What did you enjoy most about your time at [Company Name]?

(Open-ended question)

3. What did you find most challenging about your time at [Company Name]?

(Open-ended question)

**Section 2: Communication and Feedback**

4. How would you rate the communication from your supervisor/manager during your employment?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor
e) Very poor

5. Did you receive regular feedback on your performance and goals?

a) Yes, regularly
b) Yes, occasionally
c) No, rarely
d) No, never

6. Were you satisfied with the frequency and quality of feedback you received?

a) Yes
b) Mostly
c) Neutral
d) Mostly not
e) No

**Section 3: Job Satisfaction and Engagement**

7. How satisfied were you with your job overall?

a) Very satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat dissatisfied
e) Very dissatisfied

8. Did you feel engaged and motivated in your work?

a) Yes, most of the time
b) Sometimes
c) Rarely
d) Never

9. What factors contributed to your job satisfaction (check all that apply)?

(Select all that apply)

* Sense of accomplishment
* Opportunities for growth and development
* Collaborative work environment
* Recognition and rewards
* Other (please specify)

**Section 4: End of Working Relationship**

10. How would you rate the process of ending your working relationship with [Company Name]?

a) Smooth and efficient
b) Somewhat smooth
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat challenging
e) Very challenging

11. Were you satisfied with the support and resources provided during the transition period?

a) Yes
b) Mostly
c) Neutral
d) Mostly not
e) No

12. Do you have any suggestions for improving the end of working relationship process at [Company Name]?

(Open-ended question)

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback. Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our processes and provide a better experience for our employees.

Please note that this is just a sample questionnaire, and you may want to modify it based on your specific needs and goals.

**Career Path Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We're interested in understanding your career aspirations and experiences within our organization. Your feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and create opportunities for growth and development.

**Section 1: Current Role and Satisfaction**

1. What is your current job title and department?
2. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current role? (1 = Very Dissatisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)
3. What are the most enjoyable aspects of your current role?
4. What are the most challenging aspects of your current role?

**Section 2: Career Goals and Aspirations**

1. What are your short-term career goals (next 1-2 years)? Are you looking to move into a new role, take on additional responsibilities, or pursue a specific project?
2. What are your long-term career aspirations (next 3-5 years)? Do you see yourself in a leadership role, switching to a different department, or pursuing a new field?
3. What skills or knowledge do you need to acquire to achieve your career goals?
4. Are there any specific industries, sectors, or companies that interest you?

**Section 3: Career Development and Support**

1. Have you received any formal training or mentorship within the organization? If so, what was the most valuable aspect of the experience?
2. Do you feel supported in your career development by your manager, HR, or other resources? Why or why not?
3. What types of training, workshops, or courses would you like to see offered within the organization to support your career growth?
4. Are there any specific mentors or role models within the organization who have inspired or guided you?

**Section 4: Barriers and Challenges**

1. What are the biggest barriers or challenges you face in achieving your career goals?
2. Are there any specific skills or knowledge gaps that you're aware of?
3. Do you feel that there are any biases or obstacles within the organization that might impact your career advancement?
4. Are there any specific policies or procedures that you think need to be improved or changed to support career development?

**Section 5: Additional Comments and Suggestions**

1. Is there anything else you'd like to share about your career aspirations or experiences within the organization?
2. Do you have any suggestions for improving the organization's support for career development or employee growth?
3. Are there any specific initiatives or programs that you think would be beneficial for employees looking to advance their careers?

Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and experiences! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a more supportive and growth-oriented environment.

**Access to Technology and Tools Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve our work processes and employee experience, we would like to gather your thoughts and opinions on access to technology and tools within the company. c) Occasionally
d) Rarely

a) Email
b) Microsoft Office (Word, Excel, PowerPoint, etc.)
c) Collaboration tools (e.g. Slack, Trello, Asana)
d) Project management software (e.g. Jira, Basecamp)
e) Other (please specify)

a) Yes, please specify
b) No

**Section 2: Barriers to Technology and Tool Adoption**

a) Lack of training or support
b) Technical issues or compatibility problems
c) Limited access or availability
d) Resistance to change or unfamiliarity with new tools
e) Other (please specify)

2. Have you ever experienced any of the following issues when trying to use technology and tools?

a) Slow or unreliable internet connection
b) Difficulty navigating or finding the right tool
c) Limited functionality or features
d) Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Suggestions for Improvement**

1. What would you like to see improved or changed about our technology and tool infrastructure?

a) More training or support
b) Easier navigation or user interface
c) More features or functionality
d) Increased accessibility or availability
e) Other (please specify)

2. Are there any new technologies or tools that you think would be beneficial to the company or your role?

a) Yes, please specify
b) No

	* Other (please specify)

**Employee Motivation Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We're interested in understanding what drives and motivates our employees to achieve their best work. Your input will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more engaging and fulfilling work environment. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to elaborate on your responses.

**Section 1: Job Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current job?

(1 = Very dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat satisfied, 5 = Very satisfied)

2. What are the most important factors that contribute to your job satisfaction? (Select all that apply)

a) Meaningful work and sense of purpose
b) Opportunities for growth and development
c) Recognition and rewards
d) Collaborative and supportive work environment
e) Autonomy and flexibility
f) Other (please specify)

3. Have you experienced a significant change in your job satisfaction over the past 6 months? If so, what triggered the change?

**Section 2: Motivators and Demotivators**

4. What motivates you to come to work every day? (Select all that apply)

a) Sense of accomplishment and achievement
b) Desire to learn and grow professionally
c) Opportunity to work with a great team
d) Recognition and appreciation from management
e) Sense of responsibility and ownership
f) Other (please specify)

5. What demotivates you at work? (Select all that apply)

a) Lack of autonomy and control
b) Unclear expectations and goals
c) Limited opportunities for growth and development
d) Poor communication and feedback
e) Unsupportive or unengaged colleagues
f) Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Engagement and Commitment**

6. How committed are you to your current role and organization? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 = Not at all committed and 5 = Extremely committed)

7. What would make you more committed to your role and organization? (Select all that apply)

a) Clear goals and expectations
b) Opportunities for advancement and growth
c) Recognition and rewards for outstanding performance
d) Improved work-life balance
e) More autonomy and flexibility
f) Other (please specify)

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

8. Is there anything that you think would improve your motivation and job satisfaction? If so, please describe.

9. Are there any changes or initiatives that you think would positively impact employee motivation and engagement? If so, please describe.

Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your input is invaluable in helping us understand what drives and motivates our employees.

**Section 1: Current Feedback Mechanisms**

1. How often do you currently receive feedback from your supervisor or manager?

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Quarterly
e) Rarely

a) Performance feedback
b) Constructive criticism
c) Recognition and praise
d) Suggestions for improvement
e) Other (please specify)

a) Regular meetings
b) Email or instant messaging
c) Performance reviews
d) Anonymous feedback mechanisms
e) Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Feedback Mechanisms Effectiveness**

1. How effective do you think our current feedback mechanisms are in helping you grow and develop in your role?

a) Very effective
b) Somewhat effective
c) Not very effective
d) Not at all effective

2. Do you feel that your feedback is regularly acted upon and implemented?

a) Yes
b) Sometimes
c) Rarely
d) Never

3. Are there any specific feedback mechanisms that you feel are missing or underutilized?

**Section 3: Desired Feedback Mechanisms**

1. What types of feedback would you like to receive more frequently?

a) Performance feedback
b) Constructive criticism
c) Recognition and praise
d) Suggestions for improvement
e) Other (please specify)

2. Would you prefer to receive feedback in a more formal or informal setting?

a) Formal (e.g. performance reviews)
b) Informal (e.g. regular check-ins)
c) Both formal and informal

3. Are there any specific feedback mechanisms that you would like to see implemented in the future?

**Conclusion:**

              {"ANSWER": "Open-ended feedback"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Note that I've used the `TYPE_ID` property to specify the type of question, and the `_TF_ANSWERS` property to specify the possible answers for each question.

**Internal Mobility Opportunities Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for participating in this survey! Your input will help us understand the current state of internal mobility opportunities within our organization and identify areas for improvement. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**Section 1: Current Job Satisfaction and Mobility Aspirations**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current job?

(1 = Very Dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Satisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)

2. How often do you think about exploring new opportunities within the company?

(1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost Always, 5 = Always)

3. What motivates you to consider internal mobility opportunities? (Select all that apply)

* Career growth and development
* New challenges and responsibilities
* Desire to work in a different department or team
* Better work-life balance
* Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Barriers to Internal Mobility**

1. What do you think is the biggest obstacle to exploring internal mobility opportunities? (Select all that apply)

* Lack of awareness about available opportunities
* Limited job openings or competition for positions
* Fear of change or uncertainty
* Concerns about job security or stability
* Other (please specify)

2. Have you ever felt discouraged from pursuing internal mobility opportunities due to:

* Lack of support from management or HR
* Limited resources or training for new roles
* Concerns about being seen as a "job hopper"
* Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Preferred Internal Mobility Channels**

1. Which of the following channels would you prefer to learn about internal mobility opportunities? (Select all that apply)

* Company-wide announcements or newsletters
* Departmental or team meetings
* Social media or internal communication platforms
* One-on-one conversations with managers or HR representatives
* Other (please specify)

2. Would you prefer to receive internal mobility opportunities through:

* Job postings or job descriptions
* Mentorship or coaching programs
* Professional development workshops or training sessions
* Networking events or internal conferences
* Other (please specify)

**Section 4: Additional Comments and Suggestions**

1. Do you have any suggestions for improving internal mobility opportunities within our organization?

2. Are there any specific skills or training you would like to see offered to support internal mobility?

3. Is there anything else you would like to share about your experiences or aspirations regarding internal mobility?

Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a more mobile and engaged workforce.

**Leadership Effectiveness Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve leadership development, we would like to gather your feedback on the effectiveness of our leaders. Your input will help us identify areas of strength and opportunities for growth. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**Section 1: Leadership Style**

1. How would you describe the leadership style of our managers?

a) Autocratic
b) Democratic
c) Transformational
d) Other (please specify)

2. Do you feel that our leaders are approachable and open to feedback?

a) Always
b) Most of the time
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely

3. How would you rate the level of trust you have in our leaders?

a) High
b) Medium
c) Low

**Section 2: Communication**

4. How would you rate the communication style of our leaders?

a) Clear and concise
b) Somewhat clear, but sometimes confusing
c) Not very clear
d) Not at all clear

5. Do you feel that our leaders keep you informed about important changes or initiatives?

a) Yes, always
b) Yes, most of the time
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely

6. How would you rate the frequency of feedback from our leaders?

a) Regularly
b) Occasionally
c) Rarely
d) Never

**Section 3: Decision-Making**

7. How would you rate the decision-making process of our leaders?

a) Collaborative and inclusive
b) Somewhat collaborative, but sometimes decisive
c) Decisive, but not always collaborative
d) Autocratic

8. Do you feel that our leaders involve you in decision-making processes?

a) Always
b) Most of the time
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely

9. How would you rate the level of transparency in our leaders' decision-making?

a) High
b) Medium
c) Low

**Section 4: Employee Engagement**

Here is a sample questionnaire on Onboarding Experience:

**Onboarding Experience Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We value your feedback and want to understand your experience during the onboarding process. Your input will help us improve our onboarding program and ensure that new hires have a smooth transition into our organization. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**Section 1: Pre-Onboarding**

1. How did you first learn about our company and the job opportunity?
	* I saw the job posting on our website
	* I saw the job posting on a job board or career website
	* I was referred by a current employee or friend
	* I saw an advertisement on social media
	* Other (please specify)
2. How would you rate the clarity of the job description and requirements?
	* Very clear
	* Somewhat clear
	* Not very clear
	* Not at all clear
3. Did you have any questions or concerns about the job or company before starting the onboarding process?
	* Yes
	* No

**Section 2: Onboarding Process**

1. How would you rate the overall onboarding experience?
	* Excellent
	* Good
	* Fair
	* Poor
2. Were you provided with a comprehensive onboarding plan or checklist?
	* Yes
	* No
3. How would you rate the quality of the training and orientation provided?
	* Excellent
	* Good
	* Fair
	* Poor
4. Were you introduced to your new colleagues and supervisor during the onboarding process?
	* Yes
	* No
5. Did you feel supported and guided throughout the onboarding process?
	* Yes
	* No

**Section 3: Job Knowledge and Skills**

1. How would you rate your understanding of the job responsibilities and expectations?
	* Excellent
	* Good
	* Fair
	* Poor
2. Have you received adequate training and support to perform your job duties?
	* Yes
	* No
3. Do you feel confident in your ability to perform your job duties?
	* Yes
	* No

**Section 4: Additional Comments and Suggestions**

1. What did you find most helpful or enjoyable about the onboarding process?
2. What did you find most challenging or frustrating about the onboarding process?
3. Do you have any suggestions for improving the onboarding process?

**Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our onboarding program.**

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample questionnaire on Onboarding Experience:

**Onboarding Experience Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us improve our onboarding process. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to elaborate on your responses.

**Section 1: Pre-Onboarding Experience**

1. How did you learn about our company's job opening?
	* Online job board
	* Social media
	* Referral from current employee or friend
	* Job fair or recruitment event
	* Other (please specify)
2. What were your expectations about the onboarding process before starting your new role?
	* I was unsure what to expect
	* I expected a formal orientation program
	* I expected to learn the basics of the job and company culture
	* I expected to be thrown into the deep end and figure things out on my own
	* Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Onboarding Process**

1. How would you rate the overall onboarding experience?
	* Excellent
	* Good
	* Fair
	* Poor
2. What was the most helpful aspect of the onboarding process?
	* Meeting with my supervisor or manager
	* Learning about company culture and values
	* Completing paperwork and HR tasks
	* Meeting with HR or other departments
	* Other (please specify)
3. What was the most challenging part of the onboarding process?
	* Learning new software or systems
	* Meeting new people and building relationships
	* Understanding company policies and procedures
	* Feeling overwhelmed with too much information
	* Other (please specify)
4. How often did you feel supported or guided during the onboarding process?
	* Most of the time
	* Sometimes
	* Rarely
	* Never

**Section 3: Post-Onboarding Experience**

1. How would you rate your overall job satisfaction since onboarding?
	* Very satisfied
	* Somewhat satisfied
	* Neutral
	* Somewhat dissatisfied
	* Very dissatisfied
2. Have you experienced any difficulties or challenges in your role since onboarding?
	* Yes, but I've been able to overcome them
	* Yes, and I'm still struggling
	* No, everything has been smooth sailing
3. How likely are you to recommend our company as a great place to work?
	* Very likely
	* Somewhat likely
	* Neutral
	* Somewhat unlikely
	* Very unlikely

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

1. Do you have any suggestions for improving the onboarding process?
2. Is there anything you wish you had known before starting your new role?
3. Any additional comments or feedback about your onboarding experience?

Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our onboarding process.

	* Poor

	* No

	* Yes
	* No
	* Partially (please specify)

	* Good

	* Poor

	* Yes
	* No
	* Partially (please specify)

	* (Open-ended text box)

**Section 5: Overall Satisfaction**

	* Somewhat satisfied
	* Neutral
	* Somewhat dissatisfied
	* Very dissatisfied

**Recognition and Rewards Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We're interested in understanding your thoughts and opinions on recognition and rewards within our organization. Your feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and develop strategies to recognize and reward our employees' hard work and achievements.

**Section 1: Current Recognition and Rewards Practices**

1. How often do you feel recognized and rewarded for your work?

a) Frequently (daily/weekly)
b) Occasionally (monthly/quarterly)
c) Rarely (annually or less)
d) Never

2. What types of recognition and rewards do you value most? (Select all that apply)

a) Public recognition (e.g., company-wide announcements, awards)
b) Monetary rewards (e.g., bonuses, gift cards)
c) Non-monetary rewards (e.g., extra time off, flexible work arrangements)
d) Other (please specify)

3. Have you ever received a recognition or reward that motivated you to continue working hard? If so, what was it?

**Section 2: Desired Recognition and Rewards**

1. What would you like to see more of in terms of recognition and rewards? (Select all that apply)

a) More frequent recognition
b) More meaningful rewards
c) More opportunities for employee involvement in recognition and reward decisions
d) Other (please specify)

2. Are there any specific recognition and rewards that you think would be most effective in motivating you and your colleagues?

**Section 3: Barriers to Recognition and Rewards**

1. What barriers do you think prevent employees from feeling recognized and rewarded? (Select all that apply)

a) Lack of transparency in recognition and reward processes
b) Limited opportunities for employee recognition and reward
c) Perceived favoritism or bias in recognition and reward decisions
d) Other (please specify)

2. Have you ever felt overlooked or undervalued despite your hard work and contributions? If so, what was the impact on your job satisfaction and motivation?

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

1. Do you have any suggestions for improving our recognition and rewards practices?

2. Are there any specific recognition and rewards that you think would be most effective in recognizing and rewarding our employees' hard work and achievements?

Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and opinions on recognition and rewards! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a more positive and motivating work environment.

**Introduction:**

**Section 1: Current Recognition and Rewards**

a) Frequently
b) Occasionally
c) Rarely
d) Never

2. What types of recognition do you value most? (Select all that apply)

a) Public recognition (e.g., company-wide announcements, awards)
b) Private recognition (e.g., personalized notes, emails)
c) Monetary rewards (e.g., bonuses, gift cards)
d) Non-monetary rewards (e.g., extra time off, flexible work arrangements)
e) Other (please specify)

(Open-ended text field for respondents to provide their thoughts)

a) Yes, it motivates me to strive for excellence
b) No, it creates undue stress and pressure
c) It depends on the specific metrics/goals

**Introduction:**

Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**Section 1: Current Practices**

1. How often do you work remotely or from home?
	* Daily
	* Occasionally (1-2 times a week)

	* Never

	* Better work-life balance
	* Increased productivity
	* Reduced commuting time
	* Improved focus
	* Other (please specify)

	* Yes, at a co-working space
	* No, I use public spaces or coffee shops
	* No, I don't have a dedicated workspace

**Section 2: Challenges and Opportunities**

	* Difficulty staying motivated or focused
	* Limited social interaction or feeling isolated
	* Other (please specify)

	* Not at all important

	* Improved employee satisfaction and well-being
	* Increased productivity and efficiency
	* Better work-life balance for employees

* Industry-specific knowledge

**WorkLife Balance Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey. Your responses will help us understand the current state of worklife balance within our organization and identify areas for improvement. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to elaborate on your responses if you'd like.

**Section 1: Perceptions of WorkLife Balance**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how would you rate your current worklife balance?

(1 = Very poor, 2 = Poor, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Good, 5 = Excellent)

2. Do you feel that your work demands are impacting your personal life? (Select all that apply)

a) Yes, significantly
b) Yes, somewhat
c) No, not at all

3. How often do you find yourself working outside of regular working hours (e.g., evenings, weekends, or during vacations)?

a) Frequently (more than 2 times a week)
b) Occasionally (1-2 times a week)
c) Rarely (less than 1 time a week)
d) Never

**Section 2: Time Management and Prioritization**

4. How do you prioritize your tasks and responsibilities at work?

a) I prioritize tasks based on urgency and importance
b) I prioritize tasks based on my own goals and objectives
c) I prioritize tasks based on feedback from others (e.g., manager, colleagues)

5. Do you feel that you have enough time to complete your tasks and responsibilities during regular working hours?

a) Yes, I always have enough time
b) Yes, I usually have enough time
c) No, I often feel rushed
d) No, I rarely have enough time

**Section 3: Support Systems and Resources**

6. Do you feel that your organization provides adequate support systems and resources to help you achieve a better worklife balance?

a) Yes, I feel well-supported
b) Somewhat, I feel somewhat supported
c) No, I don't feel supported

7. What would you like to see your organization do to better support worklife balance? (Open-ended question)

**Section 4: Overall Satisfaction and Recommendations**

8. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current worklife balance?

(1 = Very dissatisfied, 2 = Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Satisfied, 5 = Very satisfied)

9. Do you have any recommendations for improving worklife balance within our organization? (Open-ended question)

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey. Your input is invaluable in helping us understand the current state of worklife balance within our organization. If you have any additional comments or suggestions, please feel free to include them below.

**WorkLife Balance Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**

**Section 1: Perceptions of WorkLife Balance**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how would you rate your current WorkLife Balance?

(1 = Very Poor, 2 = Poor, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Good, 5 = Excellent)

2. Do you feel that your work schedule allows for sufficient time for personal and family responsibilities?

a) Always
b) Most of the time
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely
e) Never

3. How often do you feel overwhelmed by work-related tasks and responsibilities?

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Rarely
e) Never

**Section 2: Work-Related Factors**

4. How many hours do you typically work per week?

(Open-ended text field)

5. Do you feel that your job demands are reasonable and manageable?

a) Yes
b) Mostly
c) Somewhat
d) Not really
e) No

6. Have you experienced any changes in your work schedule or workload in the past 6 months?

a) Yes, an increase
b) Yes, a decrease
c) No change
d) Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Personal and Family Life**

7. How many hours do you typically spend on personal and family activities per week?

(Open-ended text field)

8. Do you feel that your personal and family life is impacted by your work schedule?

a) Yes, positively
b) Yes, negatively

Here's a sample questionnaire on Work-Life Balance:

**Work-Life Balance Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for participating in this survey! The purpose of this questionnaire is to understand your perceptions and experiences regarding work-life balance within our organization. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and develop strategies to support your well-being.

**Section 1: Perceptions of Work-Life Balance**

1. How would you rate your current work-life balance?

a) Excellent - I have a good balance between work and personal life.
b) Good - I'm able to manage my work and personal responsibilities effectively.
c) Fair - I sometimes feel overwhelmed by work demands, but I'm able to cope.
d) Poor - I often feel like I'm sacrificing my personal life for work.

2. Do you feel that your work schedule allows for adequate time for personal activities?

a) Yes, I have a flexible schedule that allows me to pursue personal interests.
b) Mostly, I have some flexibility, but it's not always ideal.
c) No, my schedule is too rigid, leaving little time for personal activities.
d) It depends on the project or deadline, but generally, I have some flexibility.

3. How often do you feel the need to work outside of regular working hours?

a) Rarely - I'm able to complete tasks within regular working hours.
b) Occasionally - I need to work some extra hours, but it's not frequent.
c) Frequently - I often need to work outside of regular hours to meet deadlines.
d) Almost always - I feel like I'm always working, even outside of regular hours.

**Section 2: Impact on Personal Life**

4. How has your work-life balance affected your physical health?

a) Positively - I feel more energized and healthy.
b) Neutral - My physical health is unaffected.
c) Negatively - I experience stress-related physical symptoms.
d) Very negatively - My physical health has suffered significantly.

5. How has your work-life balance affected your mental health?

a) Positively - I feel more calm and focused.
b) Neutral - My mental health is unaffected.
c) Negatively - I experience stress-related mental symptoms.
d) Very negatively - My mental health has suffered significantly.

6. Have you noticed any changes in your relationships with family and friends due to your work-life balance?

a) Yes, my relationships have improved.
b) Yes, my relationships have suffered.
c) No, my relationships remain unaffected.
d) It's a mix - some relationships have improved, while others have suffered.

**Section 3: Support and Resources**

7. Do you feel supported by your manager and colleagues in achieving a better work-life balance?

a) Yes, I feel fully supported.
b) Mostly, I feel somewhat supported.
c) Not really, I feel somewhat unsupported.
d) No, I feel completely unsupported.

8. Are there any resources or benefits that you feel would help you achieve a better work-life balance?

a) Flexible scheduling
b) Telecommuting options
c) Employee wellness programs
d) Other (please specify)

**Section 4: Suggestions and Feedback**

9. What changes would you suggest to improve work-life balance within our organization?

10. Do you have any additional feedback or comments about your work-life balance experience?

Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a more supportive and balanced work environment.

**Workload Management Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to understand how employees manage their workload and identify areas for improvement. Your responses will help us develop strategies to optimize workload management and enhance overall job satisfaction.

**Section 1: Current Workload Management Practices**

1. How do you currently prioritize your tasks and responsibilities?

a) I use a task list or planner
b) I rely on my memory and intuition
c) I prioritize based on deadlines and urgency
d) I prioritize based on importance and impact
e) Other (please specify)

2. How often do you feel overwhelmed by your workload?

a) Rarely
b) Occasionally
c) Frequently
d) Almost always

3. What tools or methods do you use to manage your workload? (Select all that apply)

a) Task management software (e.g., Trello, Asana)
b) Paper-based planners or to-do lists
c) Email filters or flags
d) Color-coding or categorization
e) Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Challenges and Stressors**

4. What are the most significant challenges you face in managing your workload? (Select all that apply)

a) Insufficient time or resources
b) Unclear priorities or expectations
c) High volume of tasks or responsibilities
d) Lack of support or collaboration
e) Other (please specify)

5. How do you typically handle stress or pressure related to your workload?

a) I take regular breaks or practice self-care
b) I seek support from colleagues or superiors
c) I re-prioritize or adjust my workload
d) I try to power through or push through
e) Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Desired Workload Management Strategies**

6. What workload management strategies or tools would you like to see implemented to improve your work experience? (Select all that apply)

a) Task automation or delegation
b) Prioritization frameworks or templates
c) Time-blocking or scheduling tools
d) Regular check-ins or progress updates
e) Other (please specify)

7. How important is it for you to have a clear understanding of your workload and priorities?

a) Very important
b) Somewhat important
c) Not very important
d) Not at all important

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

8. Do you have any suggestions or ideas for improving workload management within the organization?

9. Are there any specific pain points or areas of concern that you'd like to see addressed in workload management?

b) Occasionally
c) Frequently
d) Almost always

b) 11-20%

c) No, rarely

c) Not very important
d) Not at all important

Here's a sample questionnaire on Workplace Culture:

**Workplace Culture Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey. Your feedback is invaluable in helping us understand and improve our workplace culture. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to elaborate on your responses if you'd like.

**Section 1: Perceptions of Workplace Culture**

1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere in our workplace?

a) Friendly and collaborative
b) Formal and professional
c) Diverse and inclusive
d) Other (please specify)

2. Do you feel like you belong in our workplace?

a) Yes, I feel like I'm part of the team
b) Somewhat, I'm still getting to know people
c) Not really, I feel like an outsider
d) Unsure

3. How would you rate the level of trust among colleagues?

a) High - we trust each other
b) Medium - we're generally trustworthy
c) Low - we don't always trust each other

**Section 2: Communication and Feedback**

4. How would you rate the communication style of our leaders?

a) Clear and transparent
b) Somewhat clear, but could be improved
c) Not very clear

5. Do you feel like your opinions and ideas are valued and considered?

a) Yes, my voice is heard
b) Somewhat, but not always
c) No, my opinions are not valued

6. How often do you receive constructive feedback from your manager or colleagues?

a) Regularly - it helps me grow
b) Occasionally - it's helpful when I receive it
c) Rarely - I don't receive much feedback

**Section 3: Inclusivity and Diversity**

7. Do you feel like our workplace is inclusive and welcoming to all employees?

a) Yes, I feel included
b) Somewhat, but there's room for improvement
c) No, I don't feel included

8. Have you experienced or witnessed any biases or discrimination in the workplace?

a) Yes, I've experienced it personally
b) Yes, I've seen it happen to others
c) No, I haven't seen or experienced it

9. How important is diversity and inclusion to you in the workplace?

a) Very important - it's essential
b) Somewhat important - it's nice to have
c) Not very important - it's not a priority

**Section 4: Professional Development and Growth**

10. Do you feel like you have opportunities for professional growth and development in our workplace?

a) Yes, I have opportunities to learn and grow
b) Somewhat, but I need to seek them out
c) No, I don't see opportunities for growth

11. How would you rate the support you receive from your manager or colleagues for your career goals?

a) Excellent - I have a strong support system
b) Good - I have some support
c) Fair - I don't have much support

12. Are you satisfied with your current role and responsibilities?

a) Yes, I'm satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied, but there's room for improvement
c) No, I'm not satisfied

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey. Your feedback is invaluable in helping us understand and improve our workplace culture. If you have any additional comments or suggestions, please feel free to include them below.

I hope this helps! Let me know if you'd like me to convert it into a specific format.

**Workplace Culture Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We're interested in understanding the current state of our workplace culture and how it impacts our daily work lives. Your honest feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more positive and productive work environment.

**Section 1: Perceptions of Workplace Culture**

(1 = Very negative, 2 = Somewhat negative, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat positive, 5 = Very positive)

(Open-ended text field)

3. Do you feel like your opinions and ideas are valued and considered in our workplace?

(Yes/No)

4. How would you describe the level of trust and respect among team members?

(Scale: 1 = Low, 2 = Medium, 3 = High)

**Section 2: Communication and Feedback**

1. How often do you receive constructive feedback from your supervisor or colleagues?

(Frequency scale: Rarely, Occasionally, Frequently, Almost always)

2. Do you feel like you have a clear understanding of our company's goals and objectives?

(Yes/No)

3. How would you rate the quality of communication within our team?

(Scale: 1 = Poor, 2 = Fair, 3 = Good, 4 = Excellent)

4. Have you ever felt like your concerns or issues were ignored or dismissed?

(Yes/No)

**Section 3: Work-Life Balance and Well-being**

(Frequency scale: Rarely, Occasionally, Frequently, Almost always)

2. Do you feel like you have a healthy work-life balance?

(Yes/No)

3. How would you rate the support provided by our organization for mental health and well-being?

(Scale: 1 = Poor, 2 = Fair, 3 = Good, 4 = Excellent)

4. Have you ever felt like you were expected to work excessive hours or be available 24/7?

(Yes/No)

(Yes/No)

(Yes/No)

(Open-ended text field)

**Workplace Culture Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey. Your feedback is invaluable in helping us understand and improve our workplace culture. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide any additional comments or suggestions you may have.

**Section 1: Overall Perception**

1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere in our workplace?

a) Friendly and collaborative
b) Professional and formal
c) Challenging and competitive
d) Other (please specify)

2. Do you feel like you belong and are valued as a member of our team?

a) Strongly agree
b) Somewhat agree
c) Neither agree nor disagree
d) Somewhat disagree
e) Strongly disagree

**Section 2: Communication**

3. How would you rate the communication style of our leaders and managers?

a) Clear and transparent
b) Fairly clear, but room for improvement
c) Not very clear
d) Not at all clear

4. Do you feel like you receive regular feedback and updates on company goals and initiatives?

a) Yes, regularly
b) Sometimes, but not consistently
c) Rarely
d) Never

**Section 3: Collaboration and Teamwork**

5. How would you rate the level of collaboration and teamwork among colleagues?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

6. Do you feel like you have the support and resources you need to do your job effectively?

a) Yes, I have everything I need
b) Mostly, but there are some gaps
c) Not really, I'm struggling
d) No, I'm overwhelmed

**Section 4: Recognition and Rewards**

7. How would you rate the recognition and rewards system in our workplace?

a) Fairly effective
b) Somewhat effective, but room for improvement
c) Not very effective
d) Not at all effective

8. Do you feel like your contributions and achievements are recognized and celebrated?

a) Yes, frequently
b) Sometimes, but not consistently
c) Rarely
d) Never

**Section 5: Diversity, Equity, and Inclusion**

9. How would you rate the level of diversity, equity, and inclusion in our workplace?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

10. Do you feel like you are treated fairly and without bias in the workplace?

a) Yes, I am treated fairly
b) Mostly, but there are some exceptions
c) Not really, I've experienced bias
d) No, I've been unfairly treated

**Section 6: Additional Comments**

11. Is there anything you'd like to share about our workplace culture that isn't covered in this survey?

(Open-ended text box for respondents to provide additional feedback)

Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a positive and inclusive workplace culture.

            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 13,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": []
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Please note that I've used the same `TYPE_ID` for all questions, which is `3` (Multiple Choice). If you want to use different types, you can modify the `TYPE_ID` for each question accordingly.
